poem_Heartgem_A_ForsakenCity=
In ruins of dreams once bright and grand,Where shadows dance on broken land,
A crystal heart beats pure and true,
With hope that shall see you through.

poem_Heartgem_B_ForsakenCity=
In twilight's grip where darkness weaves,Through city streets where no one grieves,
A sapphire heart beats strong and clear,
To guide you past your deepest fear.

poem_Heartgem_C_ForsakenCity=
Where golden light pierces the night,And ancient powers shine so bright,
A gilded heart holds wisdom's key,
To set your troubled spirit free.

poem_Heartgem_D_ForsakenCity=
In realms beyond what mortals know,Where crystal energies ebb and flow,
An amethyst heart gleams with might,
To lead you through eternal night.

poem_Heartgem_A_Nightmare=
In dreams where terror holds its sway,And nightmares steal the light of day,
A crystal heart burns fierce and bright,
To banish demons from your sight.

poem_Heartgem_B_Nightmare=
Where shadows writhe and darkness creeps,And evil in the silence keeps,
A sapphire heart beats true and strong,
To right what has been proven wrong.

poem_Heartgem_C_Nightmare=
In depths where golden spirits dwell,And ancient magics weave their spell,
A golden heart shines ever true,
To see the nightmare's end come through.

poem_Heartgem_D_Nightmare=
Beyond the veil of space and time,Where mystic forces intertwine,
An amethyst heart holds the key,
To set your tortured soul set free.

poem_Heartgem_A_CelestialResort=
In halls where spirits seek their rest,And weary souls put to the test,
A crystal heart beats soft and warm,
To shelter you from every storm.

poem_Heartgem_B_CelestialResort=
Where echoes of the past remain,And memories bring joy and pain,
A sapphire heart glows bright and true,
To guide the lost souls back to you.

poem_Heartgem_C_CelestialResort=
In chambers gold where angels dwell,With stories that they'll never tell,
A golden heart holds ancient grace,
To bring peace to this sacred place.

poem_Heartgem_A_GoldenRidge=
Upon the peaks where legends soar,And winds of change blow evermore,
A crystal heart beats with the sky,
To lift your spirit ever high.

poem_Heartgem_B_GoldenRidge=
Where golden feathers catch the light,And mountain peaks reach endless height,
A sapphire heart beats strong and free,
To grant the gift of liberty.

poem_Heartgem_C_GoldenRidge=
In realms where golden eagles fly,Beneath the vast and starlit sky,
A golden heart shines ever bright,
To guide you through the darkest night.

poem_Heartgem_A_MirrorTemple=
In temples old where mirrors gleam,And nothing is quite what they seem,
A crystal heart reflects the truth,
To guard the wisdom of your youth.

poem_Heartgem_B_MirrorTemple=
Where shadows dance and mirrors break,And every step that you must take,
A sapphire heart shows what is real,
Beyond what broken spirits feel.

poem_Heartgem_C_MirrorTemple=
In halls of glass where light bends wide,And secrets have nowhere to hide,
A golden heart reveals the way,
To see beyond the light of day.

# Gym Tutorials
GYM_VOIDWALK_INTRO=
Welcome to {# 9900ff}Voidwalking{#} training!
In this technique, you'll learn to phase through void matter.
Press DASH while touching a Void Tendril to phase through it.
Timing is critical - too early or late and you'll take damage!

GYM_SOUL_SURGE_INTRO=
Welcome to {# ff6b9d}Soul Surge{#} training!
This technique channels determination into a powerful burst.
Collect 3 Soul Fragments, then press GRAB to unleash a surge.
The surge destroys nearby enemies and breaks certain barriers!

GYM_TIMELINE_HOP_INTRO=
Welcome to {# 00ffff}Timeline Hopping{#} training!
Master the art of existing in multiple timelines at once.
Time Echo Platforms phase in and out of reality.
Dash at the exact moment they're fading to sync with them!

GYM_DETERMINATION_DASH_INTRO=
Welcome to {# ff0000}Determination Dash{#} training!
The ultimate expression of will made manifest!
Chain 5 perfect dashes without touching the ground.
Each perfect dash extends your dash range by 20%!

GYM_FRIENDSHIP_COMBO_INTRO=
Welcome to {# ff88cc}Friendship Combo{#} training!
True power comes from working together.
In co-op mode, coordinate with your partner to chain abilities.
Kirby's float + Madeline's dash creates the Friendship Boost!

GYM_ULTRA_VOID_INTRO=
Welcome to {# 800000}Ultra Void Challenge{#}!
This is the ULTIMATE test of all techniques.
Combine voidwalking, soul surges, timeline hops, and more!
Only the most determined will complete this challenge!

	[SUITEDMAN right horror]
	????? ????? ?? ? ????? ??????????
	(BUT WHAT IF I TOLD YOU...)

	{pause 1.2}
	{dz_screen_glitch_heavy 0.5}
	{dz_camera_shake 1.0 violent}

	[SUITEDMAN right nightmare]
	{# ff0000}????? ????? ????? ????? ??????? ?? ?????????{#}
	{# ff0000}(YOUR NAME WAS NEVER YOURS TO CHOOSE?){#}

	{dz_jumpscare_flash 0.3}
	{dz_scream_sfx 1.0}
	{dz_screen_cut_black 0.1}

	[MADELINE left panic]
	{dz_breathing_heavy 2.0}
	What... WHAT WAS THAT?!

	{dz_fade_in 2.0 normal}
	{dz_camera_reset 1.0}
	[MADELINE left panic]
	They're... they're gone.

	[MADELINE left distracted]

	{dz_ambient_sound wind_calm 0.3}
